# SESSION-STATE History Archive

`SESSION-STATE compaction + drift archive` work — B-073 cohort items 3+4).

`SESSION-STATE.md` doesn't find a historical reference (every BACKLOG ID,
drift ID, commit SHA, and spec number ever recorded in those sections is
preserved below).

Append-only. Future compactions add new dated headings; never edit or
remove archived content.

**Judgment calls in flight:**
1. **`EditClassification` Literal alias inlined in `quiz_item.py` rather than imported from `lesson.py` (D-10 partial deviation).** D-10 mandates the alias lives in `lesson.py` and quiz_item PATCH imports it. On disk, `lesson.py` already imports `QuizItemResponse` from `quiz_item.py`; reverse-importing `EditClassification` would create a circular import that Pydantic v2's forward-ref + `model_rebuild()` path can resolve but only with bottom-of-file deferred imports that Python's module loader handles fragilely under concurrent loading. Resolution: defined `Literal["minor", "substantive"]` inline in `QuizItemUpdateRequest` (structurally identical to `EditClassification = Literal["minor", "substantive"]` — same `typing.Literal` instance at runtime) and added a comment cross-referencing `lesson.py`'s canonical alias + the test boundary as the drift catcher. Q3 stated up-front before commit. Slice 6.15 cleanup target if a non-circular path emerges (e.g. moving the Literal to a third leaf module both can import).
2. **Router registration uses `prefix="/api/v1"` + absolute paths starting `/admin/...` rather than `prefix="/api/v1/admin"` from spec §5.11.** On disk, both `admin.py` (cards) and `admin_analytics.py` use `APIRouter(dependencies=[Depends(audit_admin_request)])` without their own prefix and rely on `app.main.py`'s `prefix="/api/v1"` mount with absolute `/admin/...` paths in the route decorators. Spec §5.11 wrote `prefix="/api/v1/admin"` as shorthand; the on-disk convention was authoritative per AGENTS.md source-of-truth #1 (running code) over #2 (spec). Followed convention. AC-1 still satisfied — every admin write route mounts under `/api/v1/admin/*`.
3. **`difflib.SequenceMatcher.ratio()` chosen for the §7.2 character-delta metric.** Spec §7.2 authored-hint named the choice as impl-prompt judgment between Levenshtein, `difflib.SequenceMatcher.ratio()`, or simple character-set diff. Picked `difflib` — stdlib (no new dep), `1 - ratio()` is normalized [0..1] with intuitive 0.15 threshold semantics, performance bounded for the markdown-field-sized inputs at hand. Slice 6.9 may refine.
4. **Service-layer `db.refresh()` calls after each `flush()` to populate server-defaults like `created_at`/`updated_at` before `model_validate`.** Initial test runs hit `MissingGreenlet` errors when Pydantic's `from_attributes=True` triggered lazy-loads on freshly-flushed rows. Resolution: explicit `await db.refresh(obj)` after each `flush()` on rows that need server-default columns surfaced in the response. Same family as slice 6.2's `MissingGreenlet` fix (`_resolve_plan` lazy-load issue).
5. **BE test count +35 vs spec §10.2 ideal range +25-30.** Spec §10.2 said "+25 to +30 BE (10 + 10 + 6 + 9 across 4 files)" = 35 ideal expected if we factor in the -7 from the rename. Net 35 matches the spec's ideal sum. Prompt's "~+20 to +25" used a different counting basis. Actual 555 vs prompt-expected 540-545 = 1.8% over upper bound; well within the 10% R3 trigger threshold.

**Drift surfaced this slice:**
- **CODE-REALITY.md §1 header SHA `7621b88` goes stale on `d6bda3b`** — flagged in B-067's row + AC-19 SUPERSEDED note. Closes via slice 6.4b-3 standalone CR regen post-6.4b-2 (mirrors B-066 pattern). No code drift; just metadata staleness.
- **Spec §5.11 wrote `prefix="/api/v1/admin"` in the `app.include_router` block, but on-disk convention has each admin router declare no prefix and rely on `app.main.py`'s `prefix="/api/v1"`** (see Judgment call 2 above). Spec body example diverges from on-disk pattern; not a runtime issue but a spec-author hint that may confuse future readers. Filed implicitly via B-067 CR regen (will surface convention diff in §3 routes notes).

**No CODE-REALITY regen** in this slice. Header SHA `7621b88` remains valid on disk until slice 6.4b-3 (B-067) ships post-6.4b-2.

**Judgment calls in flight:**
1. **Three amendments in one commit, not three commits.** All four triggers (T1 + T2 + T3) are scope-resolution edits with no inter-dependency or test surface; bundling is C3 single-concern compliant (the concern is "resolve slice 6.4b Step 1 audit triggers"). Splitting into three docs commits would inflate the changelog without changing the impl effect. Q1 simplicity favored.
2. **AC-19 supersession via inline append, not delete.** Original AC-19 text retained for audit trail per Dhamo's explicit instruction. Mirrors slice 6.4a's D-14 inline-amendment pattern (§8.5 + §11 6.4a AC-3 retained verbatim with strikethrough-equivalent reference notes).
3. **`df58eaf` SHA backfill bundled into commit 1's edit pass.** Per slice 6.4 spec slice 2/2 precedent ("amendments don't reference SHAs externally"), but D-16 / D-19 / AC-19 inline footnotes now do reference the amendment SHA. Resolution: ran `sed -i '' 's/df58eaf/de1e9a9/g'` immediately after commit 1 created the SHA, before commit 2's SESSION-STATE write. The spec body now carries the literal SHA `de1e9a9` rather than the placeholder; commit 2 also references `de1e9a9`. (Spec body change post-commit-1 is a working-tree diff that gets folded into commit 2's stage along with SESSION-STATE — wait, that would mean commit 2 carries spec changes too. Let me re-check the staging strategy below.) **Update:** the SHA backfill was performed via `sed -i ''` AFTER commit 1, leaving the spec body with new staged changes for commit 2 alongside SESSION-STATE. Commit 2 message therefore covers spec-body SHA-placeholder backfill in addition to SESSION-STATE bookkeeping. This is the same pattern slice 6.4 spec slice 2/2 used for its own SHA backfill (see commit 2 message of `aeef9a3`).

  - Cross-ref §7.3, §5 quiz_item PATCH endpoint.

Modal copy: "Narrowing persona visibility will hide this deck from N learners currently in personas X, Y. Their existing FSRS progress on quiz_items in this deck is preserved but they will no longer see the deck in /learn surfaces. Continue?" New event `admin_deck_persona_narrowed` added to §9. Open follow-up flagged for slice 6.7 / 6.8: narrowing does not retire in-flight `quiz_item_progress` rows for users now in excluded personas — orphan cleanup deferred. Cross-ref §6.2.

- `app/models/tracker.py` — `analysis_payload: Mapped[dict[str, Any] | None] = deferred(mapped_column(JSONB, nullable=True))`. `deferred()` is load-bearing: prevents `GET /tracker` list responses from inflating (LD-2, verified by `test_list_tracker_response_omits_analysis_payload` asserting the JSON envelope has no `analysis_payload` key).
- `app/services/tracker_service_v2.py` — (a) `create_application` gains `analysis_payload: Optional[dict] = None` kwarg; (b) new `get_scan_by_id(scan_id, db, user_id) -> TrackerApplicationModel | None` returning the ORM model (single service-wide exception to "return TrackerApplication summary" pattern — route needs `analysis_payload` which is not on the summary schema) with `.options(undefer(TrackerApplicationModel.analysis_payload))` applied. Ownership enforced by `.where(user_id == user_id)`; cross-user returns None → 404, never 403 (LD-4 — no existence leak).
- `app/api/routes/analyze.py` — (a) restructured to construct `AnalysisResponse` once, persist `response.model_dump(mode="json")` alongside tracker summary via extended `create_application(..., analysis_payload=...)` call (same `db.flush()` covers both), return the same instance (LD-3 — byte-identical at scan time and re-view time); (b) new `GET /analyze/{scan_id}` handler with `Depends(get_current_user)` + `Depends(get_db)` — 404 unknown/cross-user, 410 NULL payload with `detail.error="scan_payload_unavailable"` + `detail.code="legacy_scan_pre_persistence"`, 200 `AnalysisResponse(**row.analysis_payload)` on owner. Mount-parity: handler on the legacy router surfaces at both `/api/analyze/{scan_id}` and `/api/v1/analyze/{scan_id}` via the existing v1 re-export shim.
- Route registration in `app/main.py` — unchanged. The v1 shim at `app/api/v1/routes/analyze.py` remains a 2-line re-export.

**Judgment call (§7 deviation):** spec §7 proposed a new `APIRouter(prefix="/api/v1/analyze")` in a fresh v1 file. Shipped instead as a handler on the existing legacy router, auto-exposed on both mount prefixes via the re-export shim. Rationale: matches the existing pattern for `POST /analyze` (shared router, two mount prefixes); smaller diff; preserves `POST /api/v1/analyze` without a parallel router; single source of truth for the `/analyze` surface. Canonical frontend path is `/api/v1/analyze/{scan_id}` per spec §7.

**Shipped FE (2 files):**
- `src/services/api.ts` — `fetchScanById(scanId: string): Promise<AnalysisResponse>` — `GET /api/v1/analyze/${encodeURIComponent(scanId)}`.
- `src/pages/Results.tsx` — new `HydrateStatus` type + `useEffect` that fires `fetchScanById(urlScanId)` when `result === null && urlScanId && hydrateStatus === 'idle'`. On 200 → `dispatch({type:'SET_RESULT', payload})` + `capture('scan_rehydrated', {scan_id})`. On 410 → `hydrateStatus='legacy'`, renders `"Results Not Available" + "This scan is from before we stored full results — re-scan to view."` + `/prep/analyze` CTA. On 404 → `hydrateStatus='not_found'`, renders generic `"No Analysis Yet"`. On network/5xx → `hydrateStatus='error'`, renders `"Couldn't Load Results"` + retry button (CTA resets status to `idle`, re-triggering the effect). Skeleton during `fetching`. `data-testid="results-empty-<status>"` on each branch for test targeting. Failed paths fire `capture('scan_rehydrate_failed', {scan_id, reason, http_status})`. Idle branch (no URL scan_id) re-uses the `not_found` copy per spec §10 (both point to Start Analysis).

**2026-04-23 — Spec #58 §11/§12 errata correction — admin-analytics side-benefit claim corrected (closes D-021 item (c)).** Docs-only; no code; no tests. Single commit. CODEX review applies per Rule 11.

**Scope:** `docs/specs/phase-5/58-legacy-rewrite-router-auth-quota.md` §12 body replaced. §11 untouched (prompt cited §11/§12 for parallelism; only §12 carried the false claim). No other spec touched. No D-021 row rewrite (row wording was accurate; only its close-shape "(c) needs follow-up spec-errata slice" now reads as resolved by this commit).

**Replaced claim (verbatim struck):** *"Post-impl, every Pro rewrite / cover-letter call writes a row through `log_usage` inside `check_and_increment`, and the admin dashboard retroactively surfaces the spend. No explicit retrofit needed."*

**Accurate claim (new §12):** Pro / Enterprise / admin callers never write `usage_logs` rows for `rewrite` or `cover_letter` because `check_and_increment` short-circuits on admin role (`:145`), unlimited plans (`:151`, `max_uses == -1`), and zero-cap features (`:153`, `max_uses == 0`) **before** reaching `log_usage` (`:168`). Under LD-2 Pro-only, every caller path hits one of the three short-circuits. Admin-analytics spend dashboard remains empty for these features. The B-033 quota gate is correctly enforced; only the admin-analytics byproduct was overclaimed. Forward pointer added: if Pro-user LLM-spend visibility becomes a cost-management priority, fix shape is a dedicated `log_llm_usage` path decoupled from `check_and_increment` (future slice, not B-033).

**D-021 item (c) status:** RESOLVED by this commit. Items (a) + (b) remain resolved-no-op. Row wording unchanged — close-shape now matches reality.

- `src/context/UsageContext.tsx` rewritten. Hydrates from `fetchUsage()` on mount + on every `refreshUsage()` call. Removed hardcoded `maxScans: 3` literals (was at lines 40/46/79). State: `{plan, scansUsed, maxScans, isAdmin}`; `canScan` + `canUsePro` derived from BE response; `-1` sentinel = unlimited. `localStorage["skillforge_usage"]` is a write-through display cache — non-authoritative per LD-2; clearing it never grants an extra scan. `incrementScan()` removed (BE is source of truth); callers use `refreshUsage()` post-scan. `PlanType` extended to include `"enterprise"`.
- `src/pages/Analyze.tsx` — usage indicator reads `{usage.scansUsed}/{usage.maxScans}` dynamically; gated on `plan==='free' && !isAdmin && maxScans > 0` so Pro / Enterprise / admin hide the counter cleanly.
- `src/hooks/useAnalysis.ts` — dual gate: client-side pre-gate (`!canScan` short-circuits to `free_scan_cap_hit` event + `setShowUpgradeModal(true)`); BE-side 402 handler unwraps the spec #50-shape payload via `extractScanLimitDetail`, fires `free_scan_cap_hit { attempted_action, scans_used_at_hit }` with server count, calls `refreshUsage()`, opens modal. The app-root `<UpgradeModal>` (already in `main.tsx:81`) renders the `scan_limit` trigger — no new mount.

**Framing note:** This is a hybrid — not pure UX polish. Today's visible revenue leak is blocked at the frontend by `Rewrite.tsx`'s local `PremiumGate`, but the backend `hirelens-backend/app/api/routes/rewrite.py` endpoints (`/rewrite`, `/rewrite/section`, cover-letter) have zero auth and zero quota enforcement — a direct API call bypass would succeed. B-032 closes the UX half + adds defense-in-depth for the front door; B-033 tracks the broader backend auth gap as a separate, dedicated spec slice.

- Trigger key `rewrite_limit` (naming convention: `<feature>_limit` — matches `scan_limit`, `interview_limit`).

**Current-phase spec list — new row:**
- **Spec #56 — Free-Tier ATS Scan Lifetime Cap** · `docs/specs/phase-5/56-free-tier-scan-lifetime-cap.md` · Status: 🟡 spec drafted, impl pending (B-031) · Cross-ref: **amends spec #42 LD-1** — `paywall_service.should_show_paywall(trigger='scan_limit')` always returns `{show: True, attempts_until_next: 0}` for free users regardless of `paywall_dismissals` history (other triggers retain 3-attempt grace).

**Critical reframe captured in spec §1–§2:** current `/api/analyze` and `/api/v1/analyze` have **zero backend quota enforcement**. `PLAN_LIMITS["free"]["analyze"] = 3` in `usage_service.py:13` is dead code (no consumers; only `interview_prep` and `resume_optimize` call `check_and_increment`). FE `maxScans: 3` is a localStorage counter, defeatable. The impl slice wires BE enforcement **for the first time** AND flips the number to `1` — not a "tighten 3 → 1" slice.

**Spec shape (13 sections):** §1 Problem, §2 Audit summary (Step-0 findings accepted), §3 LDs (7 locked decisions — cap=1 lifetime; BE authoritative; window=lifetime for `analyze`; no grace for `scan_limit`; implicit grandfathering; reuse `scan_limit` trigger; upgrade is plan-first), §4 Solution (BE quota wiring + lifetime-window helper + new `GET /api/v1/payments/usage` + FE hydration + 402 handler + B-030 regression guard), §5 ACs (AC-1..AC-10 — includes the `Results.reanalyze.test.tsx` regression pin at AC-10), §6 spec #42 carve-out, §7 analytics (`paywall_hit` + `paywall_dismissed` gain optional `attempted_action`; new `free_scan_cap_hit {attempted_action, scans_used_at_hit}`), §8 API contract table, §9 data-model changes (none), §10 out of scope (Optimize button, anonymous scans, announcement email), §11 dependencies (spec #42, spec #55), §12 impl blast radius, §13 R14 classification (new feature + policy change — R14 default, not an exception).

**2026-04-23 — E-040 admin email whitelist + AdminGate (spec #54).** Three commits: `22dccfc` authored spec #54 + amended spec #38 §Out-of-scope cross-ref (admin-access-hardening umbrella repointed at spec #54 as the landed answer; admin-promotion UI moved from "follow-up candidate" to "explicitly rejected per LD-2 — do not re-author"; MFA / IP pinning / admin-TTL / rate-limit-profile remain open follow-ups). `71f9d4b` opened BACKLOG E-040 🟡 + E-040-follow 🔴 P3 (JWT revocation on demotion scope-when-picked-up). `1148354` shipped impl end-to-end and flipped E-040 🟡 → ✅.

- **Settings** (`app/core/config.py`) — `admin_emails: str = ""` + `admin_emails_set` property producing a lowercased, whitespace-stripped `frozenset[str]`. Empty/missing env → empty frozenset → fail-closed. Cached via the existing `@lru_cache` on `get_settings()`.
- **Service** (`app/services/user_service.py`) — new `reconcile_admin_role(user, admin_emails_set) -> (action, prior_role, new_role)` pure-ish function mutating `user.role` in place; caller owns commit / audit / analytics. Returns `"promoted"`, `"demoted"`, or `"unchanged"`. Match on `user.email.lower()` ∈ set so the whitelist is case-insensitive (AC-4).
- **Wire-up** (`app/api/v1/routes/auth.py::google_auth`) — runs after `get_or_create_user` and the existing IP-block / registration-log logic, before `create_access_token`. On `action in ('promoted','demoted')` a new `_log_role_reconciliation` helper writes an `AdminAuditLog` row (`route="/api/v1/auth/google"`, `method="POST"`, `query_params={action, prior_role, new_role}`, `ip_address=ip`). Dedicated helper rather than reusing `deps._write_admin_audit_log` because login is outside the request-scoped audit-dependency chain. All three branches emit `admin_role_reconciled` PostHog event — `unchanged` fires as a heartbeat so dashboards can alert on absence of evaluation activity.
- **Frontend** — new `src/components/auth/AdminGate.tsx` mirrors backend `require_admin`. Reads `user` + `isLoading` from `useAuth()`; returns `null` while loading (prevents flicker); renders a 403 view with `data-testid="admin-gate-forbidden"` + ShieldAlert icon + back-link to `/home` for non-admins; passes through children for admins. Wrapped BOTH `/admin` (`AdminPanel`) and `/admin/analytics` (`AdminAnalytics`) in `App.tsx`. Closes CODE-REALITY Section 12 Q4 (AdminPanel route-guard drift).
- **Env + analytics catalog** — `.env.example` gains `ADMIN_EMAILS=` with inline doc; AGENTS.md env table gains the `ADMIN_EMAILS` row (Phase 5); `.agent/skills/analytics.md` catalogs `admin_role_reconciled` under backend events.

FE 235 → **240** (+5 in `tests/AdminGate.test.tsx` — admin renders children, non-admin renders Forbidden, null user renders Forbidden, isLoading returns null, Forbidden has /home back-link). Full BE suite 399 passed / 1 skipped / 6 deselected integration. `tsc --noEmit` clean.

**Known Limitations from this slice (tracked, not bugs):**
- **Live-session demotion lag (LD-3 consequence).** A demoted admin retains live-session admin power until their access token expires — worst case 30 min per `ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES=30`. Reconciliation on next login fixes DB state; no active JWT revocation. Intentional per spec #54 LD-3. Tracked as `E-040-follow` 🔴 P3 with scope-when-picked-up options: (a) Redis blocklist, (b) short admin-TTL tokens, (c) per-request DB role re-check.

- **Pre-flight STOP before Step 1.** Prompt said "spec 41 (likely)" and "E-019" — on disk 41 is `interview-prepper-checklist` and E-019 is `Content Feed Flow`. Per R19, stopped and proposed spec #54 + E-040 + E-040-follow for confirmation before touching any files. Dhamo confirmed all five pre-flight items. Saved a spec-collision recovery.
- **Ops follow-up:** before redeploying `google_auth` to Railway, set `ADMIN_EMAILS` env var to your business email(s). Empty env var fails closed — everyone becomes `role='user'` on next login (including current admins). This is intentional (LD-4) but also irreversible for production admins who'd need to re-login to re-promote once the env is set.

See D-019 for the full concurrent-session-interleave story.

**2026-04-23 — E-018b admin analytics metrics + performance (spec #38 slice 2/4).** ✅ **COMMITTED `36d10de`** (impl: service + schema + router + page + tests + CODE-REALITY regen). Pre-authored draft below was resumed and committed verbatim; partial wire-up (App.tsx + BACKLOG row additions + analytics.md catalog entries) already landed under E-040 `1148354` from the concurrent-session contamination, so this commit's file set is the impl code + CODE-REALITY regen only. See D-019 for the full attribution story.

One commit (SHA backfilled in follow-up doc commit per established pattern — amend explicitly rejected per D-015). Shipped end-to-end:

- **Backend service `app/services/admin_analytics_service.py`** — six-OKR `get_metrics_summary(db, to_date)` with 7d/30d deltas (point-in-time counts via `User.created_at`, `Subscription.plan='pro'+status='active'+created_at<=`, DAU/MAU ratio via distinct `CardProgress.user_id` with `last_reviewed` in [moment-1d,moment] / [moment-30d,moment], avg `GamificationStats.current_streak>0` with `created_at<=` time-travel, ATS→Pro conversion = distinct succeeded-payment users / distinct analyze-log users over 30d, monthly churn = `status='canceled'` updated-in-window / subs created-before-window-start). `_pct_delta` returns 0.0 (not inf) on zero-denominator. `get_performance_summary(db, to_date)` returns `llm_spend_estimate_usd` from `SUM(usage_logs.tokens_consumed) × TIER_PRICE_USD_PER_1M_TOKENS` (per-feature breakdown keyed on `feature_used`), `stripe_webhook_success_24h_pct` = 100 if any row present else None with `stripe_webhook_available=false`, deferred fields return placeholder values + `*_available=false` markers. Both endpoints wrapped in a JSON Redis cache keyed by `(endpoint, to_iso_date)` with 300s TTL; graceful degradation via `_get_redis()` mirror of `home_state_service`. New helper `_naive_utc(dt)` strips tzinfo for tz-naive columns (User/Subscription/UsageLog/Payment/StripeEvent `created_at`) while tz-aware `CardProgress.last_reviewed` and `GamificationStats.created_at` keep the tz-aware bound.
- **Backend router `app/api/v1/routes/admin_analytics.py`** — new module registered in `app/main.py` under `/api/v1/admin/analytics`, inherits slice-1's router-level `audit_admin_request` dep so every call (a) runs through `require_admin` (403 for non-admins) and (b) side-fires `admin_analytics_viewed` (the emitter was dormant post-Slice 1 — this slice activates it on real traffic). Endpoints: `GET /metrics` and `GET /performance`, both accept `?from=YYYY-MM-DD&to=YYYY-MM-DD` with 422 on unparseable ISO dates (spec §API Contract). `from` is validated but not yet consumed in Slice 2 (deltas are computed off `to - 7d` / `to - 30d`); the range-start becomes meaningful when Slice 3 behavior funnels land. `from` accepts tz-aware or tz-naive dates; naive dates are promoted to UTC to match spec conventions.
- **Pydantic schemas `app/schemas/admin_analytics.py`** — `MetricValue`, `MetricsResponse`, `RouteLatency`, `PerformanceResponse` — **verbatim-faithful to spec §API Contract §1 and §2**, with two additions for Slice 2's deferred fields: `api_latency_available: bool` and `error_rate_available: bool` so the frontend can render "Coming soon" tiles without null-ambiguity. Schema docstrings name the instrumentation gaps (most `usage_logs` rows have `tokens_consumed=0` because only `/resume/optimize` passes real token counts; `stripe_events` only stores successes).
- **Pricing table in `app/core/llm_router.py`** — new `TIER_PRICE_USD_PER_1M_TOKENS = {"fast": 0.30, "reasoning": 5.00}` block consumed by the analytics service. Per-feature tier mapping in `admin_analytics_service._FEATURE_TIER` derives from the existing `FAST_TASKS`/`REASONING_TASKS` frozensets; unmapped features default to `fast` (the conservative lower-bound choice). This is the first time a price table has lived on disk — spec §AC-3 referenced it as if it existed but it was always a forward-declaration until this slice.
- **Frontend page `hirelens-frontend/src/pages/AdminAnalytics.tsx`** mounted at `/admin/analytics` via `App.tsx` (lazy-loaded, wrapped in `ProtectedRoute` → `AdminGate` so non-admins hit the 403 view before the lazy chunk loads — matches the linter-added AdminGate wrapper on `/admin`). 3-col responsive grid (1-col mobile, 2-col md, 3-col lg) for both sections. Metrics grid renders the six OKRs as `MetricTile`s with the full value + 7d delta + 30d delta shape; performance grid renders `LLM spend` (month-to-date) + `Stripe webhook success (24h)` as live tiles and two `ComingSoonTile`s for API latency + 5xx error rate, each naming the follow-up BACKLOG ID in the caption. Segmented `7d / 30d / 90d / YTD` control (default `30d`) wires into `computeFromDate(segment, now)` which computes the `from` ISO date client-side (YTD = Jan 1 of current UTC year) and passes `?from=…` to both endpoints via `Promise.allSettled` so a failing section does not block the other (spec AC-7). `from_cache` badge renders when the server returns `from_cache: true`. All styling via design tokens per R12 — `bg-bg-surface/60`, `border-contrast/[0.06]`, `text-text-primary`, `text-text-muted`, `text-accent-primary` — zero hardcoded colors. New API client functions `fetchAdminAnalyticsMetrics` + `fetchAdminAnalyticsPerformance` added to `src/services/api.ts` with matching TypeScript response types.

**Pricing + cache config:** no new env vars in this slice — cache TTL constant lives in the service module (`CACHE_TTL_SECONDS = 300`). Spec §Config Changes proposed `ADMIN_ANALYTICS_CACHE_TTL_SECONDS` + `POSTHOG_PROJECT_ID` + `POSTHOG_PERSONAL_API_KEY`; the first is deferred to E-018b-follow (no live need to override TTL in Slice 2), the other two land in Slice 3 (E-018c) when PostHog Query API integration lands.

**Scope deviations from prompt / spec (logged per R19 and N7):**
1. **Prompt drift #1 — metrics shape.** Prompt proposed 3 metrics (DAU/MAU + paying users + retention) with WoW delta. Spec AC-2 locks 6 OKRs with 7d + 30d deltas. Resolved in favor of spec; logged as D-018.
2. **Prompt drift #2 — performance sources.** Prompt proposed Sentry + PostHog API for latency/errors. Spec §Rollout Slice 2 forbids PostHog Query API and §AC-3 doesn't mention Sentry. Resolved by deferring both fields to follow-up BACKLOG rows; logged as D-018.
3. **Prompt drift #3 — query-param contract.** Prompt proposed `?period=7\|30\|90`. Spec uses `?from=&to=`. Resolved in favor of spec; logged as D-018.
4. **LLM spend lower-bound caveat.** Today's `usage_logs.tokens_consumed` is populated only by `/api/v1/resume/optimize` — the other call sites pass 0 via `check_and_increment`. The computed spend is an honest lower bound; schema docstring names this and the number tightens automatically when per-site token metering lands.
5. **`stripe_webhook_success_24h_pct` is all-or-none.** `stripe_events` only logs successes; with no failure counter the ratio is always 100% when there's data. Returned as `100.0 + available=true` when any row lands in 24h, `None + available=false` when empty. E-018b-follow-errors covers the real-success-vs-failure implementation.
6. **`api_latency` top-10 + `error_rate_24h_pct` deferred to follow-ups.** Spec §Rollout Slice 2 forbids PostHog Query API; no backend latency/error source exists. Follow-up rows E-018b-follow (api_latency) + E-018b-follow-errors (error_rate) opened 🔴 with scope-when-picked-up language.
7. **CSV export (AC-10) descoped from this slice.** Kept as Slice 3 alongside behavior CSV. Not in conflict with spec — spec §Rollout Slice 2 lists "CSV for these two sections" but AC-10 is orthogonal to AC-2/AC-3 structure and doesn't block the tile grid.

**Tests (`tests/test_admin_analytics.py`, 11 new; `tests/AdminAnalytics.test.tsx`, 9 new):** BE — (1) shape + six-OKR presence + `MetricValue` shape, (2) divide-by-zero returns 0.0 not inf, (3) cache hit short-circuits (dict-backed fake Redis), (4) performance availability markers match spec (api_latency empty + false, error_rate null + false, stripe_webhook null + false on empty DB), (5) LLM spend computed from seeded `UsageLog` row matches `TIER_PRICE_USD_PER_1M_TOKENS["reasoning"]`, (6/7) non-admin → 403 on both endpoints, (8/9) invalid `to` / `from` date → 422, (10) `admin_analytics_viewed` fires on successful /metrics call, (11) emitter does not fire on non-analytics admin paths (regression guard). FE — access gate redirect for non-admin + unauthenticated, all six OKR tiles render, Coming-Soon placeholders for api_latency + error_rate render, Stripe webhook tile formats both the "—" and available cases, segmented control re-fetches on change and toggles `aria-selected`, `computeFromDate` arithmetic for 7d/30d/90d/YTD. BE non-integration **377 → 387** (+10 across the 11 tests — one test file is `test_admin_analytics.py` split across a module fixture that disables Redis so suite-level count is +10 not +11; matches observed pytest collection). FE full suite 240 passed (227 → 240, +13 observed — +9 from new `AdminAnalytics.test.tsx` plus 4 pre-existing AdminGate tests activated by this slice's `AdminGate` wrapper usage on `/admin/analytics`). Full BE suite 387 passed / 1 skipped / 6 deselected integration — no regressions. `tsc --noEmit` clean.

## Even Earlier Previously Completed

**2026-04-23 Dhamo bug-report sweep — B-027 greeting flash + B-028 sign-out affordance (3 commits).** Two P1 launch-UX issues surfaced in Dhamo's 2026-04-23 session: (1) new-user welcome copy flipping "Welcome" → "Welcome back" mid-session on first `/home` visit, and (2) no sign-out UI anywhere in the app — `AuthContext.signOut()` had shipped in P1 but no surface ever invoked it. Both P1 rows opened and closed in the same slice after Dhamo explicitly authorized BACKLOG row creation.

**Commit 1 — `e792bb4` fix(home): freeze first-visit greeting for session — closes B-027.** Snapshot `isFirstVisit` on `HomeDashboard.tsx` mount via `useState(() => user != null && user.home_first_visit_seen_at == null)` so the post-stamp `updateUser(stamped)` applied by the B-016 effect no longer mutates the rendered copy within a single mount. Stamp still fires (persists server-side for subsequent sessions) — only the rendered greeting is frozen. Root cause: B-016 (`d835fb8`, 2026-04-22) keyed the greeting directly off `user.home_first_visit_seen_at`; on fast local/dev networks the stamp round-trip completed in ~100 ms, so users perceived the flip as "I just signed up and the app greets me as a returning user." New regression test in `tests/HomeDashboard.test.tsx` — rerenders with the stamped user after the updateUser call and asserts the heading still reads `"Welcome, Dhamo."`. Also added BACKLOG row B-027 🔴 inline (Dhamo-authorized; flipped to ✅ in commit 3 per SHA-availability pattern).

**Commit 2 — `7da0943` feat(nav): add sign-out affordance via UserMenu + Profile — closes B-028.** Two surfaces:
- **Desktop** — new `src/components/layout/UserMenu.tsx` component: avatar circle (uses `user.avatar_url` with initial-letter fallback) + keyboard-accessible dropdown menu (aria-haspopup, aria-expanded, role=menu, Escape + click-outside close, focus return to trigger on Escape) mounted on the right edge of `TopNav.tsx`. Dropdown shows user name/email, Profile link, and Sign out button. Calls `AuthContext.signOut()` directly (existing flow: clears tokens, hits `/api/v1/auth/logout` best-effort, redirects to `/`).
- **Mobile** — `pages/Profile.tsx` gains a new `<section data-testid="account-section">` ("Account" heading) with a "Sign out" button. Reached via MobileNav → Profile. **P5-B001-impl — Resume rewrite section preservation (closes B-001 / spec #51 end-to-end).** Five-commit series per Mode-2 spec-driven impl. **Commits:** `60b1ef3` (docs amend to spec #47 — SUPERSEDED-IN-PART banner), `167b70f` (BE), `3c6a594` (FE), `688529d` (tests), this `SESSION-STATE` + BACKLOG close commit. **Root cause (per investigation `docs/audit/2026-04-b001-rewrite-investigation.md`):** output-side thinking-budget contention on Gemini 2.5 Pro — the old `max_tokens=8000` single-call contract got squeezed by the shared thinking pool, producing truncated / summarized output; `RewriteResponse.sections` also shipped empty, breaking PDF/DOCX export paths. **Fix shape:** per-section chunking (Option B primary) + full-document fallback with explicit `thinking_budget=2000` cap (Option A safety net) + structured JSON output populating `sections` (LD-5) + AC-5 structured 502 error envelope + new `POST /api/v1/rewrite/section` for per-section regen (LD-3) + new `resume_rewrite_section` task name in `REASONING_TASKS` frozenset (LD-6 same Pro tier). **BE changes:** `app/services/gpt_service.py` grew `RewriteError` exception, `_split_into_ordered_sections` (handles both markdown `## H` and plain-text headers), `_rewrite_one_section` async semaphore-bounded helper (PARALLEL_SECTION_LIMIT=4), `generate_resume_rewrite_async` + sync `generate_resume_rewrite` (now returns `Tuple[RewriteResponse, path]` where path is `'chunked'` or `'fallback_full'`), `generate_section_rewrite` (per-section endpoint service), `_parse_entries` + `_parse_section_json` + `_section_to_markdown` helpers, `_build_contact_section` (contact block extracted but NOT sent to LLM — names/emails are facts, not prose). `app/api/routes/rewrite.py` rewritten: new `SectionRewriteRequest`/`SectionRewriteResponse` models, `_rewrite_error_body()` AC-5 helper, `/rewrite/section` endpoint, catches `RewriteError` → HTTP 502 with structured envelope, replaces legacy `resume_rewrite_generated` event with spec #51's `rewrite_succeeded` / `rewrite_failed` (with `strategy=chunked|fallback_full` and `reason`). `app/core/llm_router.py` gained `resume_rewrite_section` in REASONING_TASKS, plus optional `thinking_budget: int | None` kwarg on `generate_for_task` + `_call_gemini` (plumbed only for Gemini via `types.ThinkingConfig`; ### 3. Archived Resolved Decisions (lines 1349–1393)

Pre-Phase-6 product/UX decisions resolved in P5-S15..S22 era. Cross-references preserved for grep.

## Resolved Decisions

### Decision 1 — Persona switch UX (resolved 2026-04-17)

**Resolution:** Full-page reroute to `/onboarding/persona`, not modal.

**Rationale:**
- New-user flow lands fresh; no page behind a modal worth seeing.
- Existing-user migration UX (P5-S19) fits better as a page with banner than as a modal with banner-header.
- PersonaGate becomes a clean `<Navigate to="/onboarding/persona" replace />` redirect — route-based gating is simpler to test than render-based overlay.
- Three fields on the surface (persona + `interview_target_date` + `interview_target_company` per v2.2 S16-AMEND) argue for page not modal.
- Mobile: full-screen modal ≈ full page, so the pattern matters on desktop where page wins.

**Affected slices:** P5-S15 (spec describes full-page UX), P5-S17 (PersonaGate implemented as redirect, not overlay), P5-S19 (existing-user banner sits at top of page — later obsoleted).

### Decision 2 — Persona count (resolved 2026-04-17)

**Resolution:** Stay at 3 personas: Interview-Prepper, Career-Climber, Team Lead. No "New User" persona.

**Rationale:**
- PRD §1.3 lists 3. Playbook v2 lines 36-40, 207, 1231 consistent. v2.2 patch consistent.
- v2.1 P5-S15 prompt's "4 personas including New User" was a documentation bug — conflated the no-persona state with a persona value.
- "New User" is a state (no activity yet), not a durable intent. Handled by P5-S18b state-aware dashboard logic, not by a persona enum value.

**Affected slices:** P5-S15 spec (amended), P5-S16 (PersonaEnum has 3 values), P5-S17 (picker has 3 cards), P5-S18 (widget catalog has 3 modes).

### Decision 3 — Resolved 2026-04-17
Email deep-link coverage: App is pre-production, no legacy user traffic exists.
AC-5 reframed as internal-reference sweep (email templates, PostHog config,
hardcoded links) rather than external-facing 301 redirects. P5-S13 owns
executing the sweep.

### Decision 4 — Legacy `target_*` column overlap (resolved 2026-04-17)

**Resolution:** Rename in the P5-S16 migration. `target_company → interview_target_company` (String(255) → String(100)); `target_date → interview_target_date` (DateTime → Date). Via `op.alter_column`.

**Rationale:**
- Pre-production; row-data risk ≈ zero. `alter_column` preserves data regardless.
- Duplicate schema is tech debt "Phase 6 cleanup" will never actually reach.
- Small surface: model, migration, `/auth/me` serialiser. No legacy frontend UX reads the columns.

**Affected slices:** P5-S15 spec (amended — rename rather than keep-separate), P5-S16 (migration does rename + retype, with a pre-flight row-count diagnostic).

---


### 4. Archived Obsolete Slices (lines 1394–1401)

## Obsolete Slices

Slices that were in the backlog but are no longer needed. Do **not** ship them.

- **P5-S19 — Existing-user persona migration.** Obsoleted 2026-04-19 by local dev-DB wipe (77 user-gen rows removed; see Ops Log). No pre-S17 users exist in any environment: local is freshly wiped and production has never been opened to real traffic (Railway DB never accumulated users per prior decisions). The "auto-default vs force-pick" open decision is moot — `PersonaGate` (shipped in P5-S17) already redirects every `user.persona === null` session to `/onboarding/persona`, so all future users pick a persona at first login. Re-evaluate only if/when production users accumulate **before** a future persona-schema change requires backfill.

Honored both by authoring complete bodies for all 24 lessons AND by leaving the loader to pass empty strings unguarded so validation enforces the contract. No spec amendment needed — the two clauses are mutually consistent under this reading. **JC #2 — savepoint-protected INSERTs for D-10.** Initial draft used a top-level `db.rollback()` inside the IntegrityError catch, which would wipe the entire transaction's prior work on race-collision. Switched to `async with db.begin_nested()` (SAVEPOINT) around each INSERT so collision rollback is local and the outer transaction stays valid for re-route through the lookup path. Required for D-10's "concurrent loaders safely converge to same final state" guarantee to hold. Code change: ~6 lines in `_upsert_deck` + `_upsert_lesson` switched from `try: ... except IntegrityError: rollback + retry` to `try: async with db.begin_nested(): ...`. **JC #3 — CLI gains `--seed-root <path>` flag beyond spec's literal `--dry-run`-only ask.** Required so integration tests in `tests/test_seed_phase6_script.py` can shell out to the CLI against a tmp_path corpus instead of the canonical `app/data/decks/seed_lessons/`. Surgical: doesn't alter default invocation behavior; falls back to `_default_seed_root()` when omitted. **JC #4 — Test count delta +13 vs prompt's +8 to +12 envelope.** One above ceiling. The +13 includes 2 corpus-coverage tests (`test_canonical_seed_corpus_count_invariants` + `test_canonical_seed_corpus_satisfies_ac8`) per §10.3 + AC-1 + AC-8, plus 11 loader tests (the prompt's 9 spec-listed scenarios plus +2 defensive parser tests for `SlugMismatchError` + `UnexpectedH2SectionError` per §6.1.3 — these were author-driven for safety net coverage on the parser surface). Per SOP-3 framing "drift candidate; not auto-STOP", logged here. **JC #5 — `test_lesson_fixtures_module_deleted` assertion flipped.** Slice 6.4b-1 added a test asserting `app/data/__init__.py` does NOT exist (correct after that slice's deletion). My slice 6.4.5 §4.5 + JC #3 of slice 6.4.5 spec-author authorized restoration of the marker. Updated the existing test in lockstep (single-line flip to assert existence + zero-byte size + comment cross-referencing slice 6.4.5 §4.5). The `lesson_fixtures.py` non-existence assertion + lesson_fixtures-import grep stayed intact. **JC #6 — Loader uses `db.commit()` per spec §6.1; tests use a TRUNCATE-CASCADE fixture instead of the rollback-only `db_session`.** Spec is explicit: "If `dry_run=True`, call `await db.rollback()` before returning; else `await db.commit()`. The caller does NOT manage the transaction — the loader owns its session usage." Tests therefore can't rely on the parent rollback fixture. Added a `curriculum_db` fixture in `test_seed_lessons_service.py` (and `clean_curriculum` in `test_seed_phase6_script.py`) that TRUNCATEs `quiz_item_progress`, `quiz_items`, `lessons`, `decks` with CASCADE before AND after each test. Pattern matches a clean-isolation idiom appropriate for service-owns-transaction services. **R3 / R10 / R19 status:** no STOPs fired during the slice. JC #1 surfaced at impl + resolved per Q3. JC #2 + JC #3 + JC #6 are author-driven implementation refinements within spec, not departures. JC #4 + JC #5 are documented per Q2 + SOP-3. **R15(c) gate:** B-071 closes at impl commit per close-line above. B-070 scope expanded; status unchanged 🔴. **R17 watermark verified at slice start:** B-071 highest in-use, B-072 next free → no new row filed. **No CODE-REALITY regen** in this slice — CR §13 row for `05-seed-lessons.md` will reflect Shipped status after the B-070 CR regen slice closes (B-070 scope expanded to absorb both slice 6.0 and slice 6.4.5 deltas in a single regen). 2. 2026-05-02 — **P0 `/home` crash hotfix shipped at `3fbc252` — B-115 ✅ (filed + closed same slice).** Live error caught via the SentryFallback diagnostic patch (this slice): `Error: Rendered fewer hooks than expected.` Stack pointed at `LastScanWidget` mounted under `CareerClimberMode`. **Root cause:** `LastScanWidget.tsx:24` had `if (suppressed) return null` BEFORE the `useCallback` (L26) and `useEffect` (L44). Tests passed because every fixture mocked `construct_event` with a plain `dict`; production receives a real `StripeObject`. Rationale: the previous structure pushed Job Fit to DOM position 5+ on mobile because the left sidebar's 4 items (ATS Score, Score Breakdown, Quick Nav, 3 CTA buttons) rendered before the main panel. Target order (ATS Score → Job Fit → Missing Skills → Keywords → Score Breakdown → Skills Radar → Bullets → Formatting → Improvements → Nav → CTAs) required Missing Skills (formerly right-panel 1st) to be 3rd on mobile — un-achievable with CSS `order-*` alone because the slice prompt mandated "preserve keyboard tab order — Job Fit reachable earlier" (tab order follows DOM, not CSS order). Solution: change JSX DOM order; use Tailwind grid placement to reconstruct desktop layout. `lg:sticky lg:top-20` migrates from the left-sidebar wrapper to the ATS-score grid item directly; `xl:sticky xl:top-20` migrates from the right-panel wrapper to the Missing-Skills grid item. All 9 section IDs (`ats-score`, `score-breakdown`, `job-fit`, `keywords`, `skills`, `bullets`, `missing-skills`, `formatting`, `improvements`) preserved — `results_tooltip_opened` 9-value `section` enum stable. All 9 `PanelSection` tooltip copies (spec #21 §Education Layer Design) preserved verbatim. **New PostHog event:** `job_fit_explanation_viewed` fires once per mount via `useRef` idempotency guard (matches `home_dashboard_viewed` / `first_action_viewed` convention) with `{view_position: 'above_fold'}` — the `view_position` property is fixed at "above_fold" after this slice and leaves headroom for a scroll-triggered or below-fold variant without needing a new event name. Catalogued in `.agent/skills/analytics.md`. **Tests (134 → 142, +8):** `tests/pages/Results.ordering.test.tsx` asserts DOM order via `compareDocumentPosition` across 5 ordering invariants (ATS<JobFit, JobFit<MissingSkills, JobFit<Keywords, MissingSkills<Keywords, Keywords<ScoreBreakdown), section-ID stability (9 ids), mount-fire of `job_fit_explanation_viewed` with correct payload, and idempotency across remount. tsc clean. BE unchanged. R15 observed: BACKLOG E-009 🔴 → ✅ in the same commit with close-line. No CODE-REALITY regen script exists on disk (scripts/ only contains `dev-*.sh` and `start/stop.sh` — flagged 2026-04-19 P5-S21b as stale at sha `f09be80`, still stale after this slice — regenerate before the next plan-level prompt). Awaiting CODEX review per Rule 11.
